== Aftermath ==

=== Formation of federal government ===
In the general election, no individual alliance won the required 112 seats needed for a majority in the [[Dewan Rakyat]] to form the next government.<ref>{{cite news |author1=Nik Nurfaqih Nik Wil |title=GE15: Hung Parliament and significance of anti-hopping law in Malaysia |url=https://www.bernama.com/en/general/news.php?id=2140918 |access-date=24 November 2022 |agency=[[Bernama]] |date=21 November 2022}}</ref>

On 19 November, Gabungan Parti Sarawak (GPS) leader [[Abang Johari]] said that his party would work together with Perikatan Nasional (PN), Barisan Nasional (BN) and Gabungan Rakyat Sabah (GRS) to form the government.<ref>{{cite news |author1=Nur Shazreena Ali |author2=Marilyn Ten |title=Abang Johari: GPS agrees to pact with PN, BN and GRS to form next government |url=https://www.theborneopost.com/2022/11/20/abang-johari-gps-agrees-to-pact-with-pn-bn-and-grs-to-form-next-government/ |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[The Borneo Post]] |date=20 November 2022}}</ref> PN leader [[Muhyiddin Yassin]] also claimed to have a sufficient majority to be appointed as prime minister, citing support from PN, BN, GPS and GRS.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.thestar.com.my/news/nation/2022/11/20/muhyiddin-i-have-the-numbers-to-be-pm|title=Muhyiddin: I have the numbers to be PM |date=20 November 2022|work=[[The Star (Malaysia)|The Star]]|access-date=21 November 2022}}</ref> However, BN leader [[Ahmad Zahid Hamidi]] said that BN had not negotiated with GPS or PN on forming a government with BN, while also stating that BN MPs already agreed to let him decide who BN would ally with to form a government.<ref>{{cite news|title=Zahid: BN never agreed to form federal govt with GPS, PN|url=https://www.nst.com.my/news/politics/2022/11/853099/zahid-bn-never-agreed-form-federal-govt-gps-pn|access-date=24 November 2022|work=[[New Straits Times]]|date=20 November 2022}}</ref>

On 20 November, In a press conference at around 3:00&nbsp;a.m. Pakatan Harapan (PH) leader [[Anwar Ibrahim]] claimed to have secured a simple majority of 111 seats a to form the next government, but refused to mention which other parties were cooperating. This came not long after Perikatan Nasional chairman Muhyiddin Yassin hinted at being able to form a coalition government but rejected working with PH.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Tan|first1=Tarrence|last2=Vethasalam|first2=Ragananthini|date=20 November 2022|title=GE15: Anwar claims simple majority, but mum on party Pakatan is cooperating with|url=https://www.thestar.com.my/news/nation/2022/11/20/ge15-anwar-claims-simple-majority-but-mum-on-party-pakatan-is-cooperating-with|work=[[The Star (Malaysia)|The Star]]|access-date=24 November 2022}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|last1=Chan|first1=Dawn|last2=Sallehudin|first2=Qistina|date=20 November 2022|title=GE15: Anwar claims PH has numbers to form govt [UPDATED]|url=https://www.nst.com.my/news/politics/2022/11/852827/ge15-anwar-claims-ph-has-numbers-form-govt-updated|work=[[New Straits Times]]|access-date=24 November 2022}}</ref>

On 21 November, PH leaders and BN leaders met at the Seri Pacific Hotel.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Chan |first1=Wai Kit |title=Anwar and Zahid among Pakatan and BN leaders at Seri Pacific Hotel in KL |url=https://www.malaymail.com/news/malaysia/2022/11/21/anwar-and-zahid-among-pakatan-and-bn-leaders-at-seri-pacific-hotel-in-kl/40964 |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[Malay Mail]] |date=21 November 2022}}</ref> Also on 21 November, the deadline for political parties to prove their majority in Parliament to form a government and nominate a prime minister was extended for 24 hours by the Yang di-Pertuan Agong, shifting the deadline to the next day.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Palansamy |first1=Yiswaree |title=Agong extends deadline for political leaders to provide numbers, PM nominees to 2&nbsp;pm tomorrow |url=https://www.malaymail.com/news/malaysia/2022/11/21/agong-extends-deadline-for-political-leaders-to-provide-numbers-pm-nominees-to-2pm-tomorrow/41021 |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[Malay Mail]] |date=21 November 2022}}</ref> Meanwhile, [[Hamzah Zainudin]] of PN said that PN submitted over 112 statutory declarations from MPs supporting Muhyiddin for prime minister.<ref>{{cite news |title=GE15: PN has submitted 'more than 112' SDs to King from MPs backing Muhyiddin for PM |url=https://www.nst.com.my/news/politics/2022/11/853330/ge15-pn-has-submitted-more-112-sds-king-mps-backing-muhyiddin-pm-nsttv |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[New Straits Times]] |date=21 November 2022}}</ref>

On 22 November, [[Ismail Sabri Yaakob]] of BN stated that BN would not support either PH or PN to form a government and was prepared to sit in opposition.<ref>{{cite web |url=https://www.nst.com.my/news/politics/2022/11/853719/ge15-ismail-sabri-bn-wont-support-any-coalition-form-federal-govt|title=GE15: Ismail Sabri: BN won't support any coalition to form federal govt|date=22 November 2022|work=New Straits Times|access-date=22 November 2022}}</ref> Meanwhile, after discontent from Sarawak over GPS working with PN, GPS stated that it was up to the Yang di-Pertuan Agong to appoint the Prime Minister; while [[Parti Warisan]] voiced support for a government with PH and BN.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Tawie |first1=Sulok |title=GPS says it is up to the Agong to decide the next prime minister |url=https://www.malaymail.com/news/malaysia/2022/11/22/gps-says-it-is-up-to-the-agong-to-decide-the-next-prime-minister/41211 |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[Malay Mail]] |date=22 November 2022}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news|date=22 November 2022|work=[[The Borneo Post]]|title=Shafie: Warisan supports PH, BN to form government|url=https://www.theborneopost.com/2022/11/22/warisan-supports-ph-bn-to-form-government/}}</ref> Also that day, the [[Istana Negara, Jalan Tuanku Abdul Halim|royal palace]] stated that after the Yang di-Pertuan Agong reviewed the nominations for prime minister, he found that "no member of parliament has the majority support to be appointed prime minister", so the Yang di-Pertuan Agong summoned Anwar and Muhyiddin to meet him.<ref>{{cite news |title=No one with simple majority, King summons Anwar and Muhyiddin |url=https://www.nst.com.my/news/politics/2022/11/853768/no-one-simple-majority-king-summons-anwar-and-muhyiddin |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[New Straits Times]] |date=22 November 2022}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Tee |first1=Kenneth |title=Anwar, Muhyiddin arrive in Istana Negara after both called by King to decide Malaysia's next govt |url=https://www.malaymail.com/news/malaysia/2022/11/22/anwar-muhyiddin-arrive-in-istana-negara-after-both-called-by-king-to-decide-malaysias-next-govt/41278 |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[Malay Mail]] |date=22 November 2022}}</ref> After the meeting, Muhyiddin said that the Yang di-Pertuan Agong proposed a [[unity government]] between Pakatan Harapan and Perikatan National, but Muhyiddin rejected it as Perikatan National "will not cooperate" with Pakatan Harapan; while Anwar acknowledged that the prime minister had yet to be determined, while stating that "given time, I think we will secure a simple majority".<ref>{{cite news |title=PN will not cooperate with PH to form government – Muhyiddin |url=https://www.bernama.com/en/politics/news.php?id=2141284 |access-date=24 November 2022 |agency=[[Bernama]] |date=22 November 2022}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=GE15: No decision yet on who will be PM, says Anwar |url=https://www.thestar.com.my/news/nation/2022/11/22/ge15-no-decision-yet-on-who-will-be-pm-says-anwar |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[The Star (Malaysia)|The Star]] |date=22 November 2022}}</ref>

On 23 November, the Yang di-Pertuan Agong met with BN and GPS leaders in the [[Istana Negara, Jalan Tuanku Abdul Halim|royal palace]].<ref>{{cite news |last1=Pei Ying |first1=Pei Ying |last2=Nizam |first2=Fuad |title=GPS convoy leaves Istana Negara |url=https://www.nst.com.my/news/politics/2022/11/854072/gps-convoy-leaves-istana-negara |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[New Straits Times]] |date=23 November 2022}}</ref> Meanwhile, some members of BN and PN met in St Regis Hotel.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Chan |first1=Dawn |title=GE15: BN asked for DPM post, sources say on BN-PN meet |url=https://www.nst.com.my/news/politics/2022/11/854296/ge15-bn-asked-dpm-post-sources-say-bn-pn-meet |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[New Straits Times]] |date=23 November 2022}}</ref>

On 24 November, [[Ahmad Maslan]] of [[United Malays National Organisation|UMNO]] stated that the party's supreme council has agreed to follow the wishes of the Yang di-Pertuan Agong for BN to join a unity government not led by PN.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Basyir |first1=Mohamed |last2=Hakim |first2=Luqman |title=GE15: Umno says no to unity government with PN |url=https://www.nst.com.my/news/politics/2022/11/854335/ge15-umno-says-no-unity-government-pn |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[New Straits Times]] |date=24 November 2022}}</ref> Meanwhile, Perikatan Nasional would consider forming a unity government, stated its secretary-general [[Hamzah Zainudin]]; while GRS leader [[Hajiji Noor]] stated that GRS would abide by the Yang di-Pertuan Agong's wishes on forming a new government, including if a unity government was formed.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Chan |first1=Julia |title=Perikatan says willing to 'consider the proposal' of unity government |url=https://www.malaymail.com/news/malaysia/2022/11/24/perikatan-says-willing-to-consider-the-proposal-of-unity-government/41683 |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[Malay Mail]] |date=24 November 2022}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=GRS will abide by Agong's decision on formation of unity govt |url=https://www.bernama.com/en/general/news.php?id=2141759 |access-date=24 November 2022 |agency=[[Bernama]] |date=24 November 2022}}</ref> Also, [[Democratic Action Party|DAP]] secretary-general [[Anthony Loke]] publicly apologised on behalf of his party to the Sarawak government and Sarawak people for any offensive statement by a DAP leader, while DAP chairman [[Lim Guan Eng]] apologised as well for "my remarks that may have offended the Sarawak Premier and the GPS Sarawak state government", calling for "a fresh start to cooperate together".<ref>{{cite news |last1=Sallehuddin |first1=Qistina |title=Lim Guan Eng finally apologises to Sarawak govt and its people |url=https://www.nst.com.my/news/nation/2022/11/854453/lim-guan-eng-finally-apologises-sarawak-govt-and-its-people |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[New Straits Times]] |date=24 November 2022}}</ref>

Later on 24 November, the [[Istana Negara, Jalan Tuanku Abdul Halim|royal palace]] announced that PH chairman [[Anwar Ibrahim]] was appointed as prime minister by the Yang di-Pertuan Agong, Al-Sultan Abdullah, after the Agong conducted a consultation with the [[Conference of Rulers]] of Malaysia.<ref name=Reuters>{{cite news |title=Malaysian opposition leader Anwar appointed prime minister |url=https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/malaysias-former-ruling-bloc-may-back-anwar-pm-race-2022-11-24/ |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[Reuters]] |date=24 November 2022}}</ref><ref name=PRU15>{{cite news |title=Anwar Ibrahim appointed as Malaysia's 10th Prime Minister |url=https://pru15.bernama.com/news-en.php?id=2141779 |access-date=24 November 2022 |agency=[[Bernama]] |date=24 November 2022}}</ref> Anwar was sworn in at 5&nbsp;pm that day, making him Malaysia's 10th prime minister.<ref name=sworn>{{cite news |title=Anwar Ibrahim sworn in as Malaysia's 10th Prime Minister |url=https://www.nst.com.my/news/nation/2022/11/854566/anwar-ibrahim-sworn-malaysias-10th-prime-minister |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[New Straits Times]] |date=24 November 2022}}</ref> However, Muhyiddin continued to insist that he had the support of a majority of 115 MPs to form the next government and called on Anwar to prove Anwar's majority; this led to former prime minister [[Najib Razak]] calling for Muhyiddin himself to prove his 115 MP majority.<ref>{{cite news |title=How about you proving your 115, Najib tells Muhyiddin |url=https://www.nst.com.my/news/politics/2022/11/854636/how-about-you-proving-your-115-najib-tells-muhyiddin |access-date=24 November 2022 |work=[[New Straits Times]] |date=24 November 2022}}</ref> As of 24 November, Anwar has received support from MPs from PH, BN, GPS, Warisan, [[Malaysian United Democratic Alliance|MUDA]] and [[Parti Bangsa Malaysia|PBM]], as well as independent MPs.<ref name=motion>{{cite news |title=Parliament session on Dec 19, motion of confidence on PM to be tabled – PM Anwar |url=https://pru15.bernama.com/news-en.php?id=2142048 |access-date=25 November 2022 |agency=[[Bernama]] |date=24 November 2022}}</ref> Anwar has pledged to hold a [[vote of confidence]] on 19 December 2022, once MPs are sworn into Parliament.<ref name=motion/>

On 25 November, both Anwar and GRS leader Hajiji Noor stated that GRS had joined the unity government, supporting Anwar; this resulted in Anwar becoming the first prime minister since [[Abdullah Ahmad Badawi]] in 2008 to have two-thirds majority support in Parliament.<ref name=good>{{cite news |last1=Dahali |first1=Rafiqah |title=GRS joined unity government for the good of Sabah, says Hajiji |url=https://www.nst.com.my/news/politics/2022/11/854997/grs-joined-unity-government-good-sabah-says-hajiji |access-date=26 November 2022 |work=[[New Straits Times]] |date=25 November 2022}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=GRS joins, unity govt achieves two-thirds of Parliament – PM Anwar |url=https://www.bernama.com/en/politics/news.php?id=2142186 |access-date=26 November 2022 |agency=[[Bernama]] |date=25 November 2022}}</ref> Meanwhile, Muhyiddin congratulated Anwar and acknowledged him as prime minister, thanked Anwar for inviting PN to join the unity government, and declined Anwar's invitation, stating that PN would play the role of a "credible opposition" to ensure "corruption-free governance".<ref name=opposition>{{cite news |last1=Rodzi |first1=Nadirah |title=PN to stay as opposition bloc, to provide checks and balances to Anwar's unity govt |url=https://www.straitstimes.com/asia/se-asia/pas-to-discuss-with-pn-on-joining-anwar-ibrahim-s-unity-government |access-date=26 November 2022 |work=[[The Straits Times]] |date=25 November 2022}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Shukry |first1=Anisah |title=A Rival's Misstep Helped Anwar Finally Land Malaysia's Top Job |url=https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2022-11-25/a-rival-s-misstep-helped-anwar-finally-land-malaysia-s-top-job |access-date=26 November 2022 |work=[[Bloomberg News]] |date=25 November 2022 |archive-url=https://archive.today/20221125101529/https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2022-11-25/a-rival-s-misstep-helped-anwar-finally-land-malaysia-s-top-job |archive-date=25 November 2022}}</ref>

Anwar Ibrahim received the vote of confidence of the parliament on 19 December.<ref>{{cite web|access-date=4 January 2023|author=Mei Mei Chu, Angie Teo|date=19 December 2022|language=en|title=Malaysia Prime Minister Anwar wins motion of confidence in parliament|url=https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/malaysia-pm-anwar-wins-motion-confidence-parliament-2022-12-19/|website=Reuters}}<!-- auto-translated by Module:CS1 translator -->.</ref>

=== International reactions ===
Following the formation of unity government and the appointment of Anwar as prime minister, organisations such as the [[European Union]],<ref name="leaders and representative">{{cite news|url=https://worldofbuzz.com/here-are-some-of-the-world-leaders-orgs-who-congratulated-anwar-ibrahim-as-10th-pm-of-malaysia/|title=Here Are Some Of The World Leaders & Orgs. Who Congratulated Anwar Ibrahim As 10th PM of Malaysia|author=Alena|work=World of Buzz|date=25 November 2022|access-date=28 November 2022}}</ref> the [[United Nations]],<ref name="leaders and representative"/> as well as various head of states and their representative including from Afghanistan,<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.nst.com.my/news/nation/2022/11/854799/india-pakistan-afghanistan-congratulate-anwar-becoming-pm|title=India, Pakistan, Afghanistan congratulate Anwar on becoming PM|work=Bernama|via=New Straits Times|date=25 November 2022|access-date=28 November 2022}}</ref> Australia,<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.nst.com.my/news/nation/2022/11/854883/australian-pm-congratulates-anwar-keen-strengthen-friendship-between|title=Australian PM congratulates Anwar, keen to strengthen friendship between nations|last=Nabila|first=Dania|work=New Straits Times|date=25 November 2022|access-date=28 November 2022}}</ref> Austria,<ref name="foreign diplomat well wishes">{{cite news|url=https://www.thestar.com.my/news/nation/2022/11/26/envoys-keen-to-work-with-new-pm|title=Envoys keen to work with new PM|last=Zainal|first=Fatimah|work=The Star|date=26 November 2022|access-date=29 November 2022}}</ref> Bahrain,<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.bna.bh/en/HRHtheCrownPrinceandthePrimeMinistercongratulatesthenewlyappointedPrimeMinisterofMalaysia.aspx?cms=q8FmFJgiscL2fwIzON1%2bDh3o4vx1FmBrHiKZI42lCZU%3d|title=HRH the Crown Prince and the Prime Minister congratulates the newly appointed Prime Minister of Malaysia|work=Bahrain News Agency|date=24 November 2022|access-date=28 November 2022}}</ref> Bangladesh,<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.dhakatribune.com/foreign-affairs/2022/11/25/sheikh-hasina-congratulates-newly-elected-malaysian-pm-anwar-ibrahim|title=Sheikh Hasina congratulates newly elected Malaysian PM Anwar Ibrahim|work=Dhaka Tribune|date=25 November 2022|access-date=28 November 2022}}</ref> Brazil,<ref name="foreign diplomat well wishes"/> Canada,<ref>{{cite news|url=https://pm.gc.ca/en/news/readouts/2022/12/13/prime-minister-justin-trudeau-speaks-prime-minister-malaysia-anwar-ibrahim|title=Prime Minister Justin Trudeau speaks with Prime Minister of Malaysia Anwar Ibrahim|work=Prime Minister of Canada|date=13 December 2022|access-date=15 December 2022}}</ref> China,<ref>{{cite news|url=http://en.people.cn/n3/2022/1126/c90000-10176670.html|title=Chinese premier sends congratulations to new Malaysian PM|last1=Jiangnan|first1=Xian|last2=Jun|first2=Liang|work=People's Daily Online|date=26 November 2022|access-date=28 November 2022}}</ref> East Timor,<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.thevibes.com/articles/uncategorized/79909/timor-leste-president-visits-anwar-at-seri-perdana|title=Timor Leste president visits Anwar at Seri Perdana|work=Bernama|via=The Vibes|date=12 December 2022|access-date=15 January 2023}}</ref> Finland,<ref name="leaders and representative"/> Germany,<ref name="foreign leaders and mission">{{cite congratulations to Datuk Seri Anwar Ibrahim, Malaysia's 10th Prime Minister|via=New Zealand High Commission in Kuala Lumpur Official Facebook Page|date=24 November 2022|access-date=29 November November 2022|access-date=28 November 2022}}</ref> Qatar,<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.qna.org.qa/en/News-Area/News/2022-11/24/0055-hh-the-amir-sends-congratulations-to-new-malaysian-prime-minister|title=HH the Amir Sends Congratulations to New Malaysian Prime 2022|access-date=2 December 2022}}</ref> Taiwan,<ref>{{cite news|url=https://taiwantoday.tw/news.php?unit=2&post=228641|title=New Malaysia PM congratulated by MOFA|work=Taiwan Today|date=25 November 2022|access-date=28 November 2022}}</ref> Turkey,<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.aa.com.tr/en/turkiye/turkish-president-congratulates-new-malaysian-premier/2747502|title=Turkish president the United Arab Emirates,<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.wam.ae/en/details/1395303105692|title=UAE leaders congratulate new Malaysian Prime Minister|last1=Esmail|first1=Esraa|last2=AlGhoul|first2=Rola|work=Emirates News Agency|date=25 November 2022|access-date=28 November 2022}}</ref> the United Kingdom,<ref name="foreign diplomat well wishes"/> the United States,<ref>{{cite press release|url=https://my.usembassy.gov/malaysias-national-elections/|title=MALAYSIA'S NATIONAL ELECTIONS [STATEMENT BY SECRETARY ANTONY J. BLINKEN]|via=United States Embassy in Malaysia|date=25 November 2022|access-date=28 November 2022}}</ref> and Yemen<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.thevibes.com/articles/news/78479/saudi-crown-prince-arab-leaders-congratulate-anwar-on-becoming-pm|title=Saudi crown prince, Arab leaders congratulate Anwar on becoming PM|work=The Vibes|date=26 November 2022|access-date=28 November 2022}}</ref> sent their congratulatory messages.

Some of the head of states of neighbouring [[ASEAN]] countries also congratulated Anwar:

*{{flag|Brunei}}: The [[Sultan of Brunei]], [[Hassanal Bolkiah]], sent a congratulatory message to Anwar Ibrahim on 25 November 2022. In the message, he expressed confidence that Anwar's leadership and integrity would allow Malaysia to enjoy "continuous development" for the prosperity of its people, and conveyed his desire to further strengthen [[Brunei–Malaysia relations|the close relations between the two countries]].<ref>{{cite news|url=https://borneobulletin.com.bn/royal-congratulatory-message-to-malaysia/|title=Royal congratulatory message to Malaysia|work=Borneo Bulletin|date=25 November 2022|access-date=27 November 2022}}</ref>
*{{flag|Indonesia}}: The [[President of Indonesia]], [[Joko Widodo]], personally congratulated Anwar Ibrahim through a telephone call on 24 November 2022. Jokowi expressed his wish to meet Anwar "as soon as possible" while Anwar reiterated that [[Indonesia]] has been "Malaysia's true ally", further adding that the [[Indonesia–Malaysia relations|two countries]] should continue to deepen economic and cultural cooperation.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://en.antaranews.com/news/262245/president-jokowi-congratulates-anwar-ibrahim-on-becoming-malaysias-pm|title=President Jokowi congratulates Anwar on becoming Malaysia's PM|last1=Assegaf|first1=Fardah|last2=Lidya N|first2=Desca|last3=Ihsan|first3=Nabil|work=Antara|date=25 November 2022|access-date=28 November 2022}}</ref>
*{{flag|Philippines}}: The [[President of the Philippines]], [[Bongbong Marcos]] extended his well wishes to Anwar Ibrahim through a tweet, describing the latter as his good friend and looking forward to the stability that Anwar's leadership provides for Malaysia as well as for the whole ASEAN region.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://mb.com.ph/2022/11/25/marcos-congratulates-new-malaysian-premier-anwar/|title=Marcos congratulates new Malaysian premier Anwar|last=Geducos|first=Argyll Cyrus|work=Manila Bulletin|date=25 November 2022|access-date=28 November 2022}}</ref>
*{{flag|Singapore}}: The [[Prime Minister of Singapore]], [[Lee Hsien Loong]], sent a congratulatory letter to Anwar Ibrahim on 24 November 2022, shortly after the Istana Negara confirmed Anwar's appointment as the new prime minister. In the letter, Lee congratulated his Pakatan Harapan coalition for their "strong performance" in the election, and noted the "[[Malaysia–Singapore relations|longstanding substantive relationship]]" between the two countries, adding that the two countries could "do much more together to enhance openness, stability and connectivity" in their bilateral relationship.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.todayonline.com/singapore/pm-lee-congratulates-anwar-ibrahim-his-appointment-malaysias-10th-prime-minister-2055741|title=PM Lee congratulates Anwar Ibrahim on his appointment as Malaysia's 10th prime minister|last=Kamil|first=Asyraf|work=[[Today (Singapore newspaper)|TODAY]] |publisher=[[Mediacorp]] |date=24 November 2022 |access-date=27 November 2022}}</ref> On 25 November, Lee called Anwar to reiterate his congratulations, and invited him to visit Singapore soon; in return, Anwar replied to Lee on [[Twitter]] that he would be looking forward to meeting him "at the earliest opportunity".<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.channelnewsasia.com/singapore/singapore-prime-minister-lee-hsien-loong-congratulate-invite-malaysia-leader-anwar-ibrahim-visit-ge15-3100341|title=PM Lee invites Malaysia's new leader Anwar to visit Singapore|work=[[CNA (TV network)|CNA]]|publisher=[[Mediacorp]]|date=25 November 2022|access-date=27 November 2022}}</ref>
*{{flag|Thailand}}: The [[Prime Minister of Thailand]], [[Prayut Chan-o-cha]], sent a congratulatory message on 4 December 2022 to Anwar on becoming the 10th prime minister of Malaysia. In the message, Prayut was looking forward with Anwar to further enhance [[Malaysia–Thailand relations|bilateral relations between the two countries]] in both regional and international levels.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.thevibes.com/articles/news/79175/anwar-thanks-thai-pm-for-message-of-congratulations|title=Anwar thanks Thai PM for message of congratulations|work=The Vibes|via=Bernama|date=4 December 2022|access-date=4 December 2022}}</ref> Earlier, the [[Deputy Prime Minister of Thailand]] and [[Ministry of Public Health (Thailand)|Health Minister]], [[Anutin Charnvirakul]] posted a congratulatory message with a video of him and Anwar through his official Facebook account on 26 November 2022. In his message, he wish "may the dual relationship of our two countries soar greater than ever before".<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.thaipost.net/general-news/271585/|title='อนุทิน' ยินดี 'อันวาร์' นั่งนายกฯ มาเลเซีย ขอความสัมพันธ์ 2 ชาติยอดเยี่ยมยิ่งขึ้น|trans-title=Anutin congratulates Anwar as Malaysia's prime minister, wishing for better relations between the two countries|language=th|work=Thai Post|date=26 November 2022|access-date=29 November 2022}}</ref>
*{{flag|Vietnam}}: The [[Prime Minister of Vietnam]], [[Pham Minh Chinh]], sent a message of congratulations to Anwar on 25 November 2022.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://en.vietnamplus.vn/congratulations-to-newlyappointed-prime-minister-of-malaysia/244476.vnp|title=Congratulations to newly-appointed Prime Minister of Malaysia|work=Vietnam News Agency|via=Vietnam+|date=25 November 2022|access-date=28 November 2022}}</ref>
